I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
OptionSelector Dim.Auto width not recalculated when Labels/Values set after construction
## Describe the bug

When using the non-generic `OptionSelector` with `Orientation = Orientation.Horizontal`, setting `Labels` and `Values` after construction doesn't trigger a width recalculation. The selector's `Dim.Auto(DimAutoStyle.Content)` (the default) computes width from the initially-empty content and never updates, so labels get truncated.

The generic `OptionSelector<TEnum>` isn't affected because it populates labels in the constructor, before the first layout pass.

## To reproduce

```csharp
using Terminal.Gui.App;
using Terminal.Gui.ViewBase;
using Terminal.Gui.Views;

var app = Application.Create();
app.Init();

using var win = new Window { Title = "Repro" };

var selector = new OptionSelector
{
    Y = 2,
    Orientation = Orientation.Horizontal,
};

// Labels set after construction (e.g. driven by a reactive binding)
selector.Labels = ["IMDb (Recommended)", "TMDb"];
selector.Values = [0, 1];

win.Add(selector);
app.Run(win);
```

**Expected:** Both labels fully visible on first render.

**Actual:** The second label is truncated (e.g. "TMDb" shows as "TM"). Navigating to the second option with arrow keys and pressing Space causes a re-layout that reveals the full text, so the data is there but the width is wrong.

## Root cause (suspected)

`SelectorBase` sets `Width = Dim.Auto(DimAutoStyle.Content)` in the constructor (line 38). The `Labels` setter calls `CreateSubViews()` which rebuilds child checkboxes, but the parent's auto width doesn't pick up the new content size until a focus-driven layout pass. Setting `Visible = false` before setting labels (common in conditional UI) makes it worse since hidden views skip layout entirely.

## Workaround

Setting `Width = Dim.Fill()` on the selector avoids the issue by not relying on content-based sizing.

## Environment

- OS: Linux (Ubuntu)
- .NET: 10.0.104
- Terminal.Gui: 2.0.0-beta.11

</pr_description>

     1	using System.Collections.Immutable;

     6	/// <summary>
     7	///     The abstract base class for <see cref="OptionSelector{TEnum}"/> and <see cref="FlagSelector{TFlagsEnum}"/>.
     8	/// </summary>
     9	/// <remarks>
    10	///     <para>Default key bindings:</para>
    11	///     <list type="table">
    12	///         <listheader>
    13	///             <term>Key</term> <description>Action</description>
    14	///         </listheader>
    15	///         <item>
    16	///             <term>Up / Left</term> <description>Moves to the previous option.</description>
    17	///         </item>
    18	///         <item>
    19	///             <term>Down / Right</term> <description>Moves to the next option.</description>
    20	///         </item>
    21	///     </list>
    22	/// </remarks>
    23	public abstract class SelectorBase : View, IOrientation, IValue<int?>
    24	{
    25	    /// <summary>
    26	    ///     Gets or sets the default Highlight Style.
    27	    /// </summary>
    28	    [ConfigurationProperty (Scope = typeof (ThemeScope))]
    29	    public static MouseState DefaultMouseHighlightStates { get; set; } = MouseState.In;
    30	
    31	    /// <summary>
    32	    ///     Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="SelectorBase"/> class.
    33	    /// </summary>
    34	    protected SelectorBase ()
    35	    {
    36	        CanFocus = true;
    37	
    38	        Width = Dim.Auto (DimAutoStyle.Content);
    39	        Height = Dim.Auto (DimAutoStyle.Content);
    40	
    41	        // ReSharper disable once UseObjectOrCollectionInitializer
    42	        _orientationHelper = new OrientationHelper (this);
    43	        _orientationHelper.Orientation = Orientation.Vertical;
    44	
    45	        // Clear all mouse bindings; the selector's SubViews will handle all
    46	        // mouse events.
    47	        MouseBindings.Clear ();
    48	
    49	        CommandsToBubbleUp = [Command.Activate, Command.Accept];
    50	
    51	        KeyBindings.ReplaceCommands (Key.CursorDown, Command.Down);
    52	        KeyBindings.ReplaceCommands (Key.CursorRight, Command.Right);
    53	        KeyBindings.ReplaceCommands (Key.CursorUp, Command.Up);
    54	        KeyBindings.ReplaceCommands (Key.CursorLeft, Command.Left);
    55	
    56	        AddCommand (Command.Down, () => MoveNext (Command.Down));
    57	        AddCommand (Command.Right, () => MoveNext (Command.Right));
    58	
    59	        AddCommand (Command.Up, () => MovePrevious (Command.Up));
    60	        AddCommand (Command.Left, () => MovePrevious (Command.Left));
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    // Stores the int value for each checkbox (replaced use of Data property)
    64	    private readonly Dictionary<CheckBox, int> _checkBoxValues = new ();
    65	
    66	    private bool MoveNext (Command command)
    67	    {
    68	        if ((command == Command.Down && Orientation == Orientation.Horizontal) || (command == Command.Right && Orientation == Orientation.Vertical))
    69	        {
    70	            return false;
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        if (Focused?.TabStop != ViewBase.TabBehavior.NoStop)
    74	        {
    75	            return false;
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        int active = SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().ToArray ().IndexOf (Focused);
    79	
    80	        if (active < SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().Count () - 1)
    81	        {
    82	            active++;
    83	        }
    84	        else
    85	        {
    86	            if (Styles.HasFlag (SelectorStyles.ShowValue))
    87	            {
    88	                _valueField?.SetFocus ();
    89	
    90	                return true;
    91	            }
    92	            active = 0;
    93	        }
    94	        SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().ToArray ().ElementAt (active).SetFocus ();
    95	
    96	        return true;
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    private bool MovePrevious (Command command)
   100	    {
   101	        if ((command == Command.Up && Orientation == Orientation.Horizontal) || (command == Command.Left && Orientation == Orientation.Vertical))
   102	        {
   103	            return false;
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        if (Focused?.TabStop != ViewBase.TabBehavior.NoStop)
   107	        {
   108	            return false;
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        int active = SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().ToArray ().IndexOf (Focused);
   112	
   113	        switch (active)
   114	        {
   115	            case -1 when Styles.HasFlag (SelectorStyles.ShowValue):
   116	                active = SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().Count () - 1;
   117	
   118	                break;
   119	
   120	            case > 0:
   121	                active--;
   122	
   123	                break;
   124	
   125	            default:
   126	                {
   127	                    if (Styles.HasFlag (SelectorStyles.ShowValue))
   128	                    {
   129	                        _valueField?.SetFocus ();
   130	
   131	                        return true;
   132	                    }
   133	                    active = SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().Count () - 1;
   134	
   135	                    break;
   136	                }
   137	        }
   138	        SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().ToArray ().ElementAt (active).SetFocus ();
   139	
   140	        return true;
   141	    }
   142	
   143	    /// <summary>
   144	    ///     Gets or sets the styles for the flag selector.
   145	    /// </summary>
   146	    public SelectorStyles Styles
   147	    {
   148	        get;
   149	        set
   150	        {
   151	            if (field == value)
   152	            {
   153	                return;
   154	            }
   155	
   156	            field = value;
   157	
   158	            CreateSubViews ();
   159	            UpdateChecked ();
   160	        }
   161	    }
   162	
   163	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   164	    protected override bool OnAccepting (CommandEventArgs args)
   165	    {
   166	        if (base.OnAccepting (args))
   167	        {
   168	            return true;
   169	        }
   170	
   171	        // Per spec: Enter key should Activate AND Accept for both OptionSelector and FlagSelector.
   172	        // Enter only triggers Command.Accept (View's default key binding), so invoke Activate here
   173	        // before continuing with Accept processing. Also handle direct programmatic Accept invocations
   174	        // (Binding is null) by activating the currently focused checkbox.
   175	        bool enterFromCheckBox = args.Context?.Binding is KeyBinding { Key: { } key }
   176	                                 && key == Key.Enter
   177	                                 && args.Context?.Source?.TryGetTarget (out View? enterSource) == true
   178	                                 && enterSource is CheckBox;
   179	
   180	        bool directAccept = args.Context?.Binding is null && Focused is CheckBox;
   181	
   182	        if (!enterFromCheckBox && !directAccept)
   183	        {
   184	            return args.Context?.Binding switch
   185	            {
   186	                { Source: { } weakSource } when weakSource.TryGetTarget (out View? src) && src == this => true,
   187	                MouseBinding mouseBinding when mouseBinding.MouseEvent!.Flags.HasFlag (MouseFlags.LeftButtonDoubleClicked) => !DoubleClickAccepts,
   188	                KeyBinding { Key: { } } keyBinding when keyBinding.Key == Key.Enter => false,
   189	                null => false,
   190	                _ => true
   191	            };
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        // Create a fresh context with Command.Activate (not Accept) and IsBubblingUp=false.
   195	        // The original args.Context may have Command=Accept and IsBubblingUp=true from a bubble,
   196	        // which would cause TryBubbleUp to bubble the wrong command to SuperView.
   197	        // For direct invocations, use the focused CheckBox as the source so OnActivated
   198	        // identifies which item to activate.
   199	        WeakReference<View> source = enterFromCheckBox ? args.Context!.Source! : new WeakReference<View> (Focused!);
   200	
   201	        CommandContext activateCtx = new (Command.Activate, source, args.Context?.Binding);
   202	        InvokeCommand (Command.Activate, activateCtx);
   203	
   204	        return args.Context?.Binding switch
   205	        {
   206	            { Source: { } weakSource } when weakSource.TryGetTarget (out View? src) && src == this => true,
   207	            MouseBinding mouseBinding when mouseBinding.MouseEvent!.Flags.HasFlag (MouseFlags.LeftButtonDoubleClicked) => !DoubleClickAccepts,
   208	            KeyBinding { Key: { } } keyBinding when keyBinding.Key == Key.Enter => false,
   209	            null => false,
   210	            _ => true
   211	        };
   212	    }
   213	
   214	    /// <summary>
   215	    ///     Gets or sets the value of the selector. Will be <see langword="null"/> if no value is set.
   216	    /// </summary>
   217	    public virtual int? Value
   218	    {
   219	        get;
   220	        set
   221	        {
   222	            if (value is { } && Values is { } && !Values.Contains ((int)value))
   223	            {
   224	                throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException (nameof (value), @$"Value must be one of the following: {string.Join (", ", Values)}");
   225	            }
   226	
   227	            if (field == value)
   228	            {
   229	                return;
   230	            }
   231	
   232	            int? previousValue = field;
   233	
   234	            // Raise IValue<int?>.ValueChanging (cancellable)
   235	            if (RaiseValueChanging (previousValue, value))
   236	            {
   237	                return;
   238	            }
   239	
   240	            Tracing.Trace.Command (this, "Value", $"{previousValue}->{value}");
   241	            field = value;
   242	
   243	            UpdateChecked ();
   244	            RaiseValueChanged (previousValue, field);
   245	        }
   246	    }
   247	
   248	    #region IValue<int?> Implementation
   249	
   250	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   251	    public event EventHandler<ValueChangedEventArgs<object?>>? ValueChangedUntyped;
   252	
   253	    /// <summary>
   254	    ///     Raises the <see cref="ValueChanging"/> event.
   255	    /// </summary>
   256	    /// <returns><see langword="true"/> if the change was cancelled.</returns>
   257	    protected bool RaiseValueChanging (int? currentValue, int? newValue)
   258	    {
   259	        ValueChangingEventArgs<int?> args = new (currentValue, newValue);
   260	        ValueChanging?.Invoke (this, args);
   261	
   262	        return args.Handled;
   263	    }
   264	
   265	    /// <summary>
   266	    ///     Raises the <see cref="ValueChanged"/> event.
   267	    /// </summary>
   268	    /// <param name="previousValue">The value before the change.</param>
   269	    /// <param name="newValue">The value after the change.</param>
   270	    protected void RaiseValueChanged (int? previousValue, int? newValue)
   271	    {
   272	        _valueField?.Text = Value.ToString ()!;
   273	
   274	        OnValueChanged (newValue, previousValue);
   275	        ValueChanged?.Invoke (this, new ValueChangedEventArgs<int?> (previousValue, newValue));
   276	        ValueChangedUntyped?.Invoke (this, new ValueChangedEventArgs<object?> (previousValue, newValue));
   277	    }
   278	
   279	    /// <summary>
   280	    ///     Called when <see cref="Value"/> has changed.
   281	    /// </summary>
   282	    protected virtual void OnValueChanged (int? value, int? previousValue) { }
   283	
   284	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   285	    public event EventHandler<ValueChangingEventArgs<int?>>? ValueChanging;
   286	
   287	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   288	    public event EventHandler<ValueChangedEventArgs<int?>>? ValueChanged;
   289	
   290	    #endregion
   291	
   292	    /// <summary>
   293	    ///     Gets or sets the option values. If <see cref="Values"/> is <see langword="null"/>, get will
   294	    ///     return values based on the <see cref="Labels"/> property.
   295	    /// </summary>
   296	    public virtual IReadOnlyList<int>? Values
   297	    {
   298	        get
   299	        {
   300	            if (field is { })
   301	            {
   302	                return field;
   303	            }
   304	
   305	            // Use Labels and assume 0..Labels.Count - 1
   306	            return Labels is { } ? Enumerable.Range (0, Labels.Count).ToList () : null;
   307	        }
   308	        set
   309	        {
   310	            field = value;
   311	
   312	            // Ensure Value defaults to the first valid entry in Values if not already set
   313	            if (Value is null && field?.Any () == true)
   314	            {
   315	                Value = field.First ();
   316	            }
   317	
   318	            CreateSubViews ();
   319	            UpdateChecked ();
   320	        }
   321	    }
   322	
   323	    /// <summary>
   324	    ///     Gets or sets the list of labels for each value in <see cref="Values"/>.
   325	    /// </summary>
   326	    public IReadOnlyList<string>? Labels
   327	    {
   328	        get;
   329	        set
   330	        {
   331	            field = value;
   332	
   333	            CreateSubViews ();
   334	            UpdateChecked ();
   335	        }
   336	    }
   337	
   338	    /// <summary>
   339	    ///     Set <see cref="Values"/> and <see cref="Labels"/> from an enum type.
   340	    /// </summary>
   341	    /// <typeparam name="TEnum">The enum type to extract from</typeparam>
   342	    /// <remarks>
   343	    ///     This is a convenience method that converts an enum to a dictionary of values and labels.
   344	    ///     The enum values are converted to int values and the enum names become the labels.
   345	    /// </remarks>
   346	    public void SetValuesAndLabels<TEnum> () where TEnum : struct, Enum
   347	    {
   348	        IEnumerable<int> values = Enum.GetValues<TEnum> ().Select (f => Convert.ToInt32 (f));
   349	        Values = values.ToImmutableList ().AsReadOnly ();
   350	        Labels = Enum.GetNames<TEnum> ();
   351	    }
   352	
   353	    // Note: AssignHotKeys and UsedHotKeys are inherited from the View base class.
   354	    // SelectorBase uses the base class's automatic hotkey assignment feature.
   355	
   356	    /// <summary>
   357	    ///     Gets or sets the tab behavior of the checkboxes within the selector. If <see cref="TabBehavior.TabStop"/> (the
   358	    ///     default),
   359	    ///     navigating within and out of the selector will follow the standard superview/subview behavior. If
   360	    ///     <see cref="TabBehavior.NoStop"/>,
   361	    ///     only the arrow keys wil navigate within the selector.
   362	    /// </summary>
   363	    public TabBehavior? TabBehavior
   364	    {
   365	        get
   366	        {
   367	            if (field is { })
   368	            {
   369	                return field;
   370	            }
   371	
   372	            return TabStop;
   373	        }
   374	        set
   375	        {
   376	            if (field == value)
   377	            {
   378	                return;
   379	            }
   380	            field = value;
   381	            CreateSubViews ();
   382	        }
   383	    }
   384	
   385	    private TextField? _valueField;
   386	
   387	    /// <summary>
   388	    ///     Creates the subviews for this selector.
   389	    /// </summary>
   390	    public virtual void CreateSubViews ()
   391	    {
   392	        // Note: UsedHotKeys cleanup is handled by the base class's RaiseSubViewRemoved
   393	        foreach (View sv in RemoveAll ())
   394	        {
   395	            // Clean up checkbox value mapping (replaced use of Data property)
   396	            if (sv is CheckBox cb)
   397	            {
   398	                _checkBoxValues.Remove (cb);
   399	            }
   400	
   401	            sv.Dispose ();
   402	        }
   403	
   404	        if (Labels is null)
   405	        {
   406	            return;
   407	        }
   408	
   409	        if (Labels?.Count != Values?.Count)
   410	        {
   411	            return;
   412	        }
   413	
   414	        for (var index = 0; index < Labels?.Count; index++)
   415	        {
   416	            Add (CreateCheckBox (Labels.ElementAt (index), Values!.ElementAt (index)));
   417	        }
   418	
   419	        if (Styles.HasFlag (SelectorStyles.ShowValue))
   420	        {
   421	            _valueField = new TextField
   422	            {
   423	                CanFocus = false,
   424	                Id = "valueField",
   425	                Text = Value.ToString ()!,
   426	
   427	                // TODO: Don't hardcode this; base it on max Value
   428	                Width = 5,
   429	                ReadOnly = true,
   430	                TabStop = TabBehavior
   431	            };
   432	
   433	            Add (_valueField);
   434	        }
   435	
   436	        // Note: Hotkey assignment is now handled automatically by the base class
   437	        // when SubViews are added via Add(). No need to call AssignUniqueHotKeys() here.
   438	        SetLayout ();
   439	    }
   440	
   441	    /// <summary>
   442	    ///     INTERNAL: Creates a checkbox subview
   443	    /// </summary>
   444	    protected CheckBox CreateCheckBox (string label, int value)
   445	    {
   446	        var checkbox = new CheckBox
   447	        {
   448	            CanFocus = true,
   449	            Title = label,
   450	            Id = label,
   451	            MouseHighlightStates = DefaultMouseHighlightStates,
   452	            TabStop = TabBehavior
   453	        };
   454	
   455	        // Store value in dictionary (replaced use of Data property)
   456	        _checkBoxValues [checkbox] = value;
   457	
   458	        return checkbox;
   459	    }
   460	
   461	    /// <summary>
   462	    ///     Gets the int value associated with a checkbox. For testing and advanced scenarios.
   463	    /// </summary>
   464	    /// <param name="checkbox">The checkbox to get the value for</param>
   465	    /// <returns>The integer value associated with the checkbox</returns>
   466	    /// <exception cref="InvalidOperationException">If the checkbox is not found or not part of this selector</exception>
   467	    public int GetCheckBoxValue (CheckBox checkbox)
   468	    {
   469	        if (_checkBoxValues.TryGetValue (checkbox, out int value))
   470	        {
   471	            return value;
   472	        }
   473	
   474	        throw new InvalidOperationException ("CheckBox value not found");
   475	    }
   476	
   477	    private int _horizontalSpace = 2;
   478	
   479	    /// <summary>
   480	    ///     Gets or sets the horizontal space for this <see cref="OptionSelector"/> if the <see cref="Orientation"/> is
   481	    ///     <see cref="Orientation.Horizontal"/>
   482	    /// </summary>
   483	    public int HorizontalSpace
   484	    {
   485	        get => _horizontalSpace;
   486	        set
   487	        {
   488	            if (_horizontalSpace == value)
   489	            {
   490	                return;
   491	            }
   492	            _horizontalSpace = value;
   493	            SetLayout ();
   494	        }
   495	    }
   496	
   497	    /// <summary>
   498	    ///     Updates the layout of the subviews based on <see cref="Orientation"/>.
   499	    /// </summary>
   500	    protected void SetLayout ()
   501	    {
   502	        var maxNaturalCheckBoxWidth = 0;
   503	
   504	        if (Values?.Count > 0 && Orientation == Orientation.Vertical)
   505	        {
   506	            maxNaturalCheckBoxWidth = SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ()
   507	                                              .Max (v =>
   508	                                                    {
   509	                                                        v.SetRelativeLayout (App?.Screen.Size ?? new Size (2048, 2048));
   510	
   511	                                                        return v.Frame.Width;
   512	                                                    });
   513	        }
   514	
   515	        for (var i = 0; i < SubViews.Count; i++)
   516	        {
   517	            if (Orientation == Orientation.Vertical)
   518	            {
   519	                SubViews.ElementAt (i).X = 0;
   520	                SubViews.ElementAt (i).Y = Pos.Align (Alignment.Start, AlignmentModes.StartToEnd);
   521	                SubViews.ElementAt (i).Margin.Thickness = new Thickness (0);
   522	                SubViews.ElementAt (i).Width = Dim.Func (_ => maxNaturalCheckBoxWidth);
   523	            }
   524	            else
   525	            {
   526	                SubViews.ElementAt (i).X = Pos.Align (Alignment.Start, AlignmentModes.StartToEnd);
   527	                SubViews.ElementAt (i).Y = 0;
   528	                SubViews.ElementAt (i).Margin.Thickness = new Thickness (0, 0, i < SubViews.Count - 1 ? _horizontalSpace : 0, 0);
   529	                SubViews.ElementAt (i).Width = Dim.Auto ();
   530	            }
   531	        }
   532	    }
   533	
   534	    /// <summary>
   535	    ///     Called when the checked state of the checkboxes needs to be updated.
   536	    /// </summary>
   537	    /// <exception cref="InvalidOperationException"></exception>
   538	    public abstract void UpdateChecked ();
   539	
   540	    /// <summary>
   541	    ///     Gets or sets whether double-clicking on an Item will cause the <see cref="View.Accepting"/> event to be
   542	    ///     raised.
   543	    /// </summary>
   544	    /// <remarks>
   545	    ///     <para>
   546	    ///         If <see langword="false"/> and Accept is not handled, the Accept event on the <see cref="View.SuperView"/> will
   547	    ///         be raised. The default is
   548	    ///         <see langword="true"/>.
   549	    ///     </para>
   550	    /// </remarks>
   551	    public bool DoubleClickAccepts { get; set; } = true;
   552	
   553	    #region IOrientation
   554	
   555	    /// <summary>
   556	    ///     Gets or sets the <see cref="Orientation"/> for this <see cref="SelectorBase"/>. The default is
   557	    ///     <see cref="Orientation.Vertical"/>.
   558	    /// </summary>
   559	    public Orientation Orientation { get => _orientationHelper.Orientation; set => _orientationHelper.Orientation = value; }
   560	
   561	    private readonly OrientationHelper _orientationHelper;
   562	
   563	#pragma warning disable CS0067 // The event is never used
   564	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   565	    public event EventHandler<CancelEventArgs<Orientation>>? OrientationChanging;
   566	
   567	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   568	    public event EventHandler<EventArgs<Orientation>>? OrientationChanged;
   569	#pragma warning restore CS0067 // The event is never used
   570	
   571	    /// <summary>Called when <see cref="Orientation"/> has changed.</summary>
   572	    /// <param name="newOrientation"></param>
   573	    public void OnOrientationChanged (Orientation newOrientation) => SetLayout ();
   574	
   575	    #endregion IOrientation
   576	}

     1	using System.Diagnostics;
     2	
     3	namespace Terminal.Gui.Views;
     4	
     5	// DoubleClick - Focus, Activate, and Accept the item under the mouse (CanFocus or not)
     6	// Click - Focus, Activate, and do NOT Accept the item under the mouse (CanFocus or not).
     7	// CanFocus - Not Focused:
     8	//  HotKey - Restore Focus. Advance Active. Do NOT Accept.
     9	//  Item HotKey - Focus item. If item is not active, make Active. Do NOT Accept.
    10	// !CanFocus - Not Focused:
    11	//  HotKey - Do NOT Restore Focus. Advance Active. Do NOT Accept.
    12	//  Item HotKey - Do NOT Focus item. If item is not active, make Active. Do NOT Accept.
    13	// Focused:
    14	//  Space key - If focused item is Active, move focus to and Activate next. Else, Activate current. Do NOT Accept.
    15	//  Enter key - Activate and Accept the focused item.
    16	//  HotKey - Restore Focus. Advance Active. Do NOT Accept.
    17	//  Item HotKey - If item is not active, make Active. Do NOT Accept. If item is active, do nothing.
    18	
    19	/// <summary>
    20	///     Provides a user interface for displaying and selecting a single item from a list of options.
    21	///     Each option is represented by a checkbox, but only one can be selected at a time.
    22	///     <see cref="OptionSelector{TEnum}"/> provides a type-safe version where a <see langword="enum"/> can be
    23	///     provided.
    24	/// </summary>
    25	public class OptionSelector : SelectorBase, IDesignable
    26	{
    27	    // By default, for OptionSelector, Value is set to 0. It can be set to null if a developer
    28	    // really wants that.
    29	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    30	    public OptionSelector () => base.Value = 0;
    31	
    32	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    33	    protected override View? GetDispatchTarget (ICommandContext? ctx)
    34	    {
    35	        // Only dispatch Activate, not Accept. Accept should bubble naturally.
    36	        if (ctx?.Command != Command.Activate)
    37	        {
    38	            return null;
    39	        }
    40	
    41	        if (ctx.Source?.TryGetTarget (out View? source) != true || source is not CheckBox cb)
    42	        {
    43	            return Focused;
    44	        }
    45	
    46	        if (ctx.Binding is { } && ctx.Binding.Commands.Contains (Command.Accept) && cb.Value == CheckState.Checked)
    47	        {
    48	            return null;
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        // When a CheckBox's activation bubbles up, the source IS the CheckBox
    52	        return source;
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    /// <summary>
    56	    ///     Consumes: OptionSelector owns selection state, not the individual CheckBoxes.
    57	    /// </summary>
    58	    protected override bool ConsumeDispatch => true;
    59	
    60	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    61	    protected override void OnActivated (ICommandContext? ctx)
    62	    {
    63	        base.OnActivated (ctx);
    64	
    65	        // Apply the value change. Runs for ALL activation paths uniformly.
    66	        // No routing-direction check needed — the framework handled dispatch/consumption.
    67	        ApplyActivation (ctx);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    /// <summary>
    71	    ///     Applies the value change based on the activation source.
    72	    /// </summary>
    73	    private void ApplyActivation (ICommandContext? ctx)
    74	    {
    75	        CheckBox? checkBox = null;
    76	
    77	        if (ctx?.Source?.TryGetTarget (out View? sourceView) == true && sourceView is CheckBox cb)
    78	        {
    79	            checkBox = cb;
    80	        }
    81	        else if (ctx?.Routing == CommandRouting.DispatchingDown && Focused is CheckBox focusedCb)
    82	        {
    83	            // External dispatch (e.g. Menu → MenuItem → OptionSelector): the DispatchingDown guard
    84	            // blocked dispatch to inner CheckBoxes. Use the currently focused CheckBox as the
    85	            // selection target — SetFocus() was called before OnActivated, so Focused is reliable.
    86	            checkBox = focusedCb;
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        if (checkBox is null)
    90	        {
    91	            Cycle ();
    92	
    93	            return;
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        if (GetCheckBoxValue (checkBox) == Value
    97	            && (ctx?.Routing == CommandRouting.DispatchingDown
    98	                || (ctx?.Binding is KeyBinding { Key: { } } keyBinding && keyBinding.Key == Key.Space)))
    99	        {
   100	            // Caused by Key.Space or a SuperView...
   101	            // If the checkbox is already checked, we cycle to the next one.
   102	            Cycle ();
   103	        }
   104	        else
   105	        {
   106	            if (Value == GetCheckBoxValue (checkBox))
   107	            {
   108	                return;
   109	            }
   110	
   111	            Value = GetCheckBoxValue (checkBox);
   112	        }
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   116	    protected override void OnSubViewAdded (View view)
   117	    {
   118	        base.OnSubViewAdded (view);
   119	
   120	        if (view is not CheckBox checkbox)
   121	        {
   122	            return;
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        checkbox.RadioStyle = true;
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    private void Cycle ()
   129	    {
   130	        int valueIndex = Values.IndexOf (v => v == Value);
   131	
   132	        Value = valueIndex == Values?.Count - 1 ? Values! [0] : Values! [valueIndex + 1];
   133	
   134	        if (HasFocus)
   135	        {
   136	            valueIndex = Values.IndexOf (v => v == Value);
   137	            SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().ToArray () [valueIndex].SetFocus ();
   138	        }
   139	
   140	        // Verify at most one is checked
   141	        Debug.Assert (SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().Count (cb => cb.Value == CheckState.Checked) <= 1);
   142	    }
   143	
   144	    /// <summary>
   145	    ///     Updates the checked state of all checkbox subviews so that only the checkbox corresponding
   146	    ///     to the current <see cref="SelectorBase.Value"/> is checked.
   147	    /// </summary>
   148	    public override void UpdateChecked ()
   149	    {
   150	        foreach (CheckBox cb in SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ())
   151	        {
   152	            int value = GetCheckBoxValue (cb);
   153	
   154	            cb.Value = value == Value ? CheckState.Checked : CheckState.UnChecked;
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        // Verify at most one is checked
   158	        Debug.Assert (SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().Count (cb => cb.Value == CheckState.Checked) <= 1);
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    /// <summary>
   162	    ///     Gets or sets the <see cref="SelectorBase.Labels"/> index for the focused item. The active item may or may not be
   163	    ///     the selected
   164	    ///     RadioItem.
   165	    /// </summary>
   166	    /// <remarks>
   167	    ///     <para>
   168	    ///         Maps to either the X or Y position within <see cref="View.Viewport"/> depending on <see cref="Orientation"/>.
   169	    ///     </para>
   170	    /// </remarks>
   171	    public int FocusedItem
   172	    {
   173	        get
   174	        {
   175	            if (!CanFocus)
   176	            {
   177	                return 0;
   178	            }
   179	
   180	            return HasFocus ? SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().ToArray ().IndexOf (Focused) : field;
   181	        }
   182	        set
   183	        {
   184	            if (!CanFocus)
   185	            {
   186	                return;
   187	            }
   188	
   189	            field = value;
   190	
   191	            CheckBox [] checkBoxes = SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().ToArray ();
   192	
   193	            if (value < 0 || value >= checkBoxes.Length)
   194	            {
   195	                throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException (nameof (value), @"FocusedItem index is out of range");
   196	            }
   197	
   198	            if (HasFocus)
   199	            {
   200	                checkBoxes [value].SetFocus ();
   201	            }
   202	        }
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   206	    public bool EnableForDesign ()
   207	    {
   208	        AssignHotKeys = true;
   209	        Labels = ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Third Option", "Option Quattro"];
   210	
   211	        return true;
   212	    }
   213	}

    public void Add (params View []? views)
    {
        if (views is null)
        {
            return;
        }

        foreach (View view in views)
        {
            Add (view);
        }
    }

    internal void RaiseSubViewAdded (View view)
    {
        // If auto-hotkey assignment is enabled, assign a hotkey to the new subview
        // This must happen BEFORE the CWP events so observers see the assigned hotkey
        if (AssignHotKeys)
        {
            AssignHotKeyToView (view);
        }

        OnSubViewAdded (view);
        SubViewAdded?.Invoke (this, new SuperViewChangedEventArgs (this, view));
    }

    internal void RaiseSubViewRemoved (View view)
    {
        // If auto-hotkey assignment is enabled, remove the subview's hotkey from UsedHotKeys
        if (AssignHotKeys && view.HotKey != Key.Empty)
        {
            UsedHotKeys.Remove (view.HotKey);
        }

        OnSubViewRemoved (view);
        SubViewRemoved?.Invoke (this, new SuperViewChangedEventArgs (this, view));
    }

     1	namespace Terminal.Gui.ViewBase;
     2	
     3	/// <summary>
     4	///     Represents a dimension that automatically sizes the view to fit all the view's Content, SubViews, and/or Text.
     5	/// </summary>
     6	/// <remarks>
     7	///     <para>
     8	///         See <see cref="DimAutoStyle"/>.
     9	///     </para>
    10	///     <para>
    11	///         See the <a href="../docs/dimauto.md">Dim.Auto Deep Dive</a> for comprehensive documentation including
    12	///         non-trivial usage patterns.
    13	///     </para>
    14	///     <para>
    15	///         SubViews that use <see cref="DimFill"/> do not contribute to the auto-sizing calculation unless
    16	///         <see cref="DimFill.MinimumContentDim"/> or <see cref="DimFill.To"/> is specified. Without either, a
    17	///         <see cref="DimFill"/> SubView will receive a size of 0 because the SuperView has no content-based size
    18	///         to fill against. Use <see cref="Dim.Fill(Dim, Dim?)"/> with a <c>minimumContentDim</c> parameter or
    19	///         <see cref="Dim.Fill(View)"/> with a <c>to</c> parameter to ensure the SubView contributes to the
    20	///         auto-sizing calculation.
    21	///     </para>
    22	///     <para>
    23	///         This is a low-level API that is typically used internally by the layout system. Use the various static
    24	///         methods on the <see cref="Dim"/> class to create <see cref="Dim"/> objects instead.
    25	///     </para>
    26	/// </remarks>
    27	/// <param name="MaximumContentDim">The maximum dimension the View's ContentSize will be fit to.</param>
    28	/// <param name="MinimumContentDim">The minimum dimension the View's ContentSize will be constrained to.</param>
    29	/// <param name="Style">The <see cref="DimAutoStyle"/> of the <see cref="DimAuto"/>.</param>
    30	public record DimAuto (Dim? MaximumContentDim, Dim? MinimumContentDim, DimAutoStyle Style) : Dim
    31	{
    32	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    33	    public override string ToString () => $"Auto({Style},{MinimumContentDim},{MaximumContentDim})";
    34	
    35	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    36	    internal override int GetAnchor (int size) => 0;
    37	
    38	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    39	    internal override bool IsFixed => true;
    40	
    41	    /// <summary>
    42	    ///     Holds categorized views for single-pass processing.
    43	    ///     Phase 1 and 2 Performance Optimization: Reduces iterations and allocations.
    44	    /// </summary>
    45	    private readonly struct ViewCategories
    46	    {
    47	        public List<View> NotDependent { get; init; }
    48	        public List<View> Centered { get; init; }
    49	        public List<View> Anchored { get; init; }
    50	        public List<View> PosViewBased { get; init; }
    51	        public List<View> DimViewBased { get; init; }
    52	        public List<View> DimAutoBased { get; init; }
    53	        public List<View> DimFillBased { get; init; }
    54	        public List<int> AlignGroupIds { get; init; }
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    /// <summary>
    58	    ///     Categorizes views in a single pass to reduce iterations and allocations.
    59	    ///     Phase 1 and 2 Performance Optimization.
    60	    /// </summary>
    61	    private static ViewCategories CategorizeViews (IList<View> subViews, Dimension dimension, int superviewContentSize)
    62	    {
    63	        ViewCategories categories = new ()
    64	        {
    65	            NotDependent = [],
    66	            Centered = [],
    67	            Anchored = [],
    68	            PosViewBased = [],
    69	            DimViewBased = [],
    70	            DimAutoBased = [],
    71	            DimFillBased = [],
    72	            AlignGroupIds = []
    73	        };
    74	
    75	        HashSet<int> seenAlignGroupIds = new ();
    76	
    77	        foreach (View v in subViews)
    78	        {
    79	            Pos pos = dimension == Dimension.Width ? v.X : v.Y;
    80	            Dim dim = dimension == Dimension.Width ? v.Width : v.Height;
    81	
    82	            // Check for not dependent views first (most common case)
    83	            if ((pos.IsFixed || dim.IsFixed) && !pos.DependsOnSuperViewContentSize && !dim.DependsOnSuperViewContentSize)
    84	            {
    85	                categories.NotDependent.Add (v);
    86	            }
    87	
    88	            // Check for centered views
    89	            if (pos.Has<PosCenter> (out _))
    90	            {
    91	                categories.Centered.Add (v);
    92	            }
    93	
    94	            // Check for anchored views
    95	            if (pos.Has<PosAnchorEnd> (out _))
    96	            {
    97	                categories.Anchored.Add (v);
    98	            }
    99	
   100	            // Check for PosView based views
   101	            if (pos.Has<PosView> (out _))
   102	            {
   103	                categories.PosViewBased.Add (v);
   104	            }
   105	
   106	            // Check for DimView based views
   107	            if (dim.Has<DimView> (out _))
   108	            {
   109	                categories.DimViewBased.Add (v);
   110	            }
   111	
   112	            // Check for DimAuto based views
   113	            if (dim.Has<DimAuto> (out _))
   114	            {
   115	                categories.DimAutoBased.Add (v);
   116	            }
   117	
   118	            // Check for DimFill based views that can contribute
   119	            if (dim.Has<DimFill> (out _) && dim.CanContributeToAutoSizing)
   120	            {
   121	                categories.DimFillBased.Add (v);
   122	            }
   123	
   124	            // Collect align group IDs
   125	            if (!pos.Has (out PosAlign posAlign))
   126	            {
   127	                continue;
   128	            }
   129	
   130	            if (seenAlignGroupIds.Add (posAlign.GroupId))
   131	            {
   132	                categories.AlignGroupIds.Add (posAlign.GroupId);
   133	            }
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        return categories;
   137	    }
   138	
   139	    /// <summary>
   140	    ///     Calculates maximum size from a pre-categorized list of views.
   141	    ///     Phase 1 and 2 Performance Optimization: Avoids redundant filtering.
   142	    /// </summary>
   143	    private static int CalculateMaxSizeFromList (List<View> views, int max, Dimension dimension)
   144	    {
   145	        foreach (View v in views)
   146	        {
   147	            int newMax = dimension == Dimension.Width
   148	                             ? v.Frame.X + v.Width.Calculate (0, max, v, dimension)
   149	                             : v.Frame.Y + v.Height.Calculate (0, max, v, dimension);
   150	
   151	            if (newMax > max)
   152	            {
   153	                max = newMax;
   154	            }
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        return max;
   158	    }
   159	
   160	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   161	    internal override int Calculate (int location, int superviewContentSize, View us, Dimension dimension)
   162	    {
   163	        var textSize = 0;
   164	        var maxCalculatedSize = 0;
   165	
   166	        // 2048 x 2048 supports unit testing where no App is running.
   167	        Size screenSize = us.App?.Screen.Size ?? new Size (2048, 2048);
   168	        int autoMin = MinimumContentDim?.GetAnchor (superviewContentSize) ?? 0;
   169	        int screenX4 = dimension == Dimension.Width ? screenSize.Width * 4 : screenSize.Height * 4;
   170	        int autoMax = MaximumContentDim?.GetAnchor (superviewContentSize) ?? screenX4;
   171	
   172	        if (Style.FastHasFlags (DimAutoStyle.Text))
   173	        {
   174	            if (dimension == Dimension.Width)
   175	            {
   176	                if (us.TextFormatter.ConstrainToWidth is null)
   177	                {
   178	                    // Set BOTH width and height (by setting Size). We do this because we will be called again, next
   179	                    // for Dimension.Height. We need to know the width to calculate the height.
   180	                    us.TextFormatter.ConstrainToSize = us.TextFormatter.FormatAndGetSize (new Size (int.Min (autoMax, screenX4), screenX4));
   181	                }
   182	
   183	                textSize = us.TextFormatter.ConstrainToWidth ?? 0;
   184	            }
   185	            else
   186	            {
   187	                // For height, we need to make sure width has been calculated.
   188	                if (us.TextFormatter.ConstrainToHeight is null)
   189	                {
   190	                    int width = int.Min (MaximumContentDim?.GetAnchor (superviewContentSize) ?? screenX4, screenSize.Width * 4);
   191	
   192	                    if (us.TextFormatter.ConstrainToWidth is null)
   193	                    {
   194	                        width = us.TextFormatter.FormatAndGetSize (new Size (us.Viewport.Width, screenX4)).Width;
   195	                    }
   196	
   197	                    textSize = us.TextFormatter.FormatAndGetSize (new Size (us.TextFormatter.ConstrainToWidth ?? width, screenX4)).Height;
   198	                    us.TextFormatter.ConstrainToHeight = textSize;
   199	                }
   200	                else
   201	                {
   202	                    textSize = us.TextFormatter.ConstrainToHeight.Value;
   203	                }
   204	            }
   205	        }
   206	
   207	        if (Style.FastHasFlags (DimAutoStyle.Content))
   208	        {
   209	            maxCalculatedSize = textSize;
   210	
   211	            if (us is { ContentSizeTracksViewport: false, InternalSubViews.Count: 0 })
   212	            {
   213	                // ContentSize was explicitly set. Use `us.ContentSize` to determine size.
   214	                maxCalculatedSize = dimension == Dimension.Width ? us.GetContentSize ().Width : us.GetContentSize ().Height;
   215	            }
   216	            else
   217	            {
   218	                // Single-pass categorization to reduce iterations and allocations
   219	                // Work directly with the collection to avoid unnecessary ToList() allocation
   220	
   221	                // Categorize views in a single pass
   222	                ViewCategories categories = CategorizeViews (us.InternalSubViews, dimension, superviewContentSize);
   223	
   224	                // Process not-dependent views
   225	                foreach (View notDependentSubView in categories.NotDependent)
   226	                {
   227	                    notDependentSubView.SetRelativeLayout (us.GetContentSize ());
   228	
   229	                    int size = dimension == Dimension.Width
   230	                                   ? notDependentSubView.X.GetAnchor (0)
   231	                                     + notDependentSubView.Width.Calculate (0, superviewContentSize, notDependentSubView, dimension)
   232	                                   : notDependentSubView.Y.GetAnchor (0)
   233	                                     + notDependentSubView.Height.Calculate (0, superviewContentSize, notDependentSubView, dimension);
   234	
   235	                    if (size > maxCalculatedSize)
   236	                    {
   237	                        maxCalculatedSize = size;
   238	                    }
   239	                }
   240	
   241	                // Process centered views
   242	                var maxCentered = 0;
   243	
   244	                foreach (View v in categories.Centered)
   245	                {
   246	                    maxCentered = dimension == Dimension.Width
   247	                                      ? v.X.GetAnchor (0) + v.Width.Calculate (0, screenX4, v, dimension)
   248	                                      : v.Y.GetAnchor (0) + v.Height.Calculate (0, screenX4, v, dimension);
   249	                }
   250	
   251	                maxCalculatedSize = int.Max (maxCalculatedSize, maxCentered);
   252	
   253	                // Process aligned views
   254	                var maxAlign = 0;
   255	
   256	                foreach (int groupId in categories.AlignGroupIds)
   257	                {
   258	                    // Convert to IReadOnlyCollection for PosAlign API
   259	                    maxAlign = PosAlign.CalculateMinDimension (groupId, us.InternalSubViews.ToArray (), dimension);
   260	                }
   261	
   262	                maxCalculatedSize = int.Max (maxCalculatedSize, maxAlign);
   263	
   264	                // Process anchored views
   265	                var maxAnchorEnd = 0;
   266	
   267	                foreach (View anchoredSubView in categories.Anchored)
   268	                {
   269	                    // Need to set the relative layout for PosAnchorEnd subviews to calculate the size
   270	                    anchoredSubView.SetRelativeLayout (dimension == Dimension.Width
   271	                                                           ? new Size (maxCalculatedSize, screenX4)
   272	                                                           : new Size (screenX4, maxCalculatedSize));
   273	
   274	                    maxAnchorEnd = dimension == Dimension.Width
   275	                                       ? anchoredSubView.X.GetAnchor (maxCalculatedSize + anchoredSubView.Frame.Width)
   276	                                       : anchoredSubView.Y.GetAnchor (maxCalculatedSize + anchoredSubView.Frame.Height);
   277	                }
   278	
   279	                maxCalculatedSize = Math.Max (maxCalculatedSize, maxAnchorEnd);
   280	
   281	                // Process PosView, DimView, and DimAuto based views
   282	                maxCalculatedSize = CalculateMaxSizeFromList (categories.PosViewBased, maxCalculatedSize, dimension);
   283	                maxCalculatedSize = CalculateMaxSizeFromList (categories.DimViewBased, maxCalculatedSize, dimension);
   284	                maxCalculatedSize = CalculateMaxSizeFromList (categories.DimAutoBased, maxCalculatedSize, dimension);
   285	
   286	                // Process DimFill views that can contribute
   287	                foreach (View dimFillSubView in categories.DimFillBased)
   288	                {
   289	                    Dim dimFill = dimension == Dimension.Width ? dimFillSubView.Width : dimFillSubView.Height;
   290	
   291	                    // Get the minimum contribution from the Dim itself
   292	                    int minContribution = dimFill.GetMinimumContribution (0, maxCalculatedSize, dimFillSubView, dimension);
   293	
   294	                    if (minContribution > 0)
   295	                    {
   296	                        // Add position offset to get total size needed
   297	                        int positionOffset = dimension == Dimension.Width ? dimFillSubView.Frame.X : dimFillSubView.Frame.Y;
   298	                        int totalSize = positionOffset + minContribution;
   299	
   300	                        if (totalSize > maxCalculatedSize)
   301	                        {
   302	                            maxCalculatedSize = totalSize;
   303	                        }
   304	                    }
   305	
   306	                    // Handle special case for DimFill with To (still needs type-specific logic)
   307	                    if (dimFill is not DimFill dimFillTyped || dimFillTyped.To is null)
   308	                    {
   309	                        continue;
   310	                    }
   311	
   312	                    // The SuperView needs to be large enough to contain both the dimFillSubView and the To view
   313	                    int dimFillPos = dimension == Dimension.Width ? dimFillSubView.Frame.X : dimFillSubView.Frame.Y;
   314	                    int toViewPos = dimension == Dimension.Width ? dimFillTyped.To.Frame.X : dimFillTyped.To.Frame.Y;
   315	                    int toViewSize = dimension == Dimension.Width ? dimFillTyped.To.Frame.Width : dimFillTyped.To.Frame.Height;
   316	                    int totalSizeTo = int.Max (dimFillPos, toViewPos + toViewSize);
   317	
   318	                    if (totalSizeTo > maxCalculatedSize)
   319	                    {
   320	                        maxCalculatedSize = totalSizeTo;
   321	                    }
   322	                }
   323	            }
   324	        }
   325	
   326	        // All sizes here are content-relative; ignoring adornments.
   327	        // We take the largest of text and content.
   328	        int max = int.Max (textSize, maxCalculatedSize);
   329	
   330	        // And, if min: is set, it wins if larger
   331	        max = int.Max (max, autoMin);
   332	
   333	        // And, if max: is set, it wins if smaller
   334	        max = int.Min (max, autoMax);
   335	
   336	        Thickness thickness = us.GetAdornmentsThickness ();
   337	
   338	        int adornmentThickness = dimension switch
   339	                                 {
   340	                                     Dimension.Width => thickness.Horizontal,
   341	                                     Dimension.Height => thickness.Vertical,
   342	                                     Dimension.None => 0,
   343	                                     _ => throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException (nameof (dimension), dimension, null)
   344	                                 };
   345	
   346	        max += adornmentThickness;
   347	
   348	        return max;
   349	    }
   350	
   351	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   352	    protected override bool HasInner<TDim> (out TDim dim)
   353	    {
   354	        if (MinimumContentDim is { } && MinimumContentDim.Has (out dim))
   355	        {
   356	            return true;
   357	        }
   358	
   359	        if (MaximumContentDim is { } && MaximumContentDim.Has (out dim))
   360	        {
   361	            return true;
   362	        }
   363	
   364	        dim = null!;
   365	
   366	        return false;
   367	    }
   368	}



2026-05-29 16:27:41,950 - INFO - swea-agent-gui-cs__Terminal.Gui-4860 - ========================= STEP 20 =========================
2026-05-29 16:27:41,954 - DEBUG - swea-lm-gui-cs__Terminal.Gui-4860 - n_cache_control: 2
2026-05-29 16:28:28,914 - DEBUG - swea-lm-gui-cs__Terminal.Gui-4860 - Response: ModelResponse(id='96f5e62a43f340ada7d20156d16e11e8', created=1780072069, model='DeepSeek-V4-Pro', object='chat.completion', system_fingerprint=None, choices=[Choices(finish_reason='tool_calls', index=0, message=Message(content='Now I understand the layout system. When `Calculate` is called for `DimAutoStyle.Content`, it iterates subviews and computes their sizes. The issue is that in the `SetLayout()` method (in `SelectorBase`), the subview widths are set to `Dim.Auto()` and `X` is set to `Pos.Align(...)`. \n\nLet me trace the problem more carefully for the horizontal case. When `SetLayout()` is called:\n- `SubViews[0].X = Pos.Align(Alignment.Start, AlignmentModes.StartToEnd)` \n- `SubViews[0].Width = Dim.Auto()`\n- `SubViews[1].X = Pos.Align(Alignment.Start, AlignmentModes.StartToEnd)`\n\nWait, `Pos.Align(Alignment.Start, AlignmentModes.StartToEnd)` - this is a position type. Let me check how this works. For horizontal layout, all items have `X = Pos.Align(Alignment.Start, ...)` and `Y = 0`. \n\nActually, looking at this more carefully, I think the issue may be that the `SetLayout()` method happens AFTER the `Add` calls but the `SetNeedsLayout()` triggered by the `Add` calls has already been scheduled. But `SetLayout()` changes the subviews\' width and positions - and these changes might not trigger another layout update.\n\nActually, I think the core issue might be simpler. 1. `RemoveAll()` - triggers `SetNeedsLayout()` on parent

3. `SetLayout()` - does NOT trigger `SetNeedsLayout()` on parent

```csharp
SubViews.ElementAt(i).Margin.Thickness = new Thickness (0, 0, i < SubViews.Count - 1 ? _horizontalSpace : 0, 0);
SubViews.ElementAt(i).Width = Dim.Auto ();
```

> Setting `Labels` and `Values` after construction doesn't trigger a width recalculation.

```csharp
    if (Value is null && field?.Any () == true)

```

So `Values` also calls `CreateSubViews()`. But `Labels` calls `CreateSubViews()` too. They can be called in any order. If `Labels` is called first without `Values` being set, `CreateSubViews` will return early because `Labels?.Count != Values?.Count`.

```csharp
selector.Values = [0, 1];
```

     1	using System.ComponentModel;
     2	
     3	namespace Terminal.Gui.ViewBase;
     4	
     5	/// <summary>
     6	///     Enables alignment of a set of views.
     7	/// </summary>
     8	/// <remarks>
     9	///     <para>
    10	///         Updating the properties of <see cref="Aligner"/> is supported, but will not automatically cause re-layout to
    11	///         happen. <see cref="View.Layout()"/>
    12	///         must be called on the SuperView.
    13	///     </para>
    14	///     <para>
    15	///         Views that should be aligned together must have a distinct <see cref="GroupId"/>. When only a single
    16	///         set of views is aligned within a SuperView, setting <see cref="GroupId"/> is optional because it defaults to 0.
    17	///     </para>
    18	///     <para>
    19	///         The first view added to the Superview with a given <see cref="GroupId"/> is used to determine the alignment of
    20	///         the group.
    21	///         The alignment is applied to all views with the same <see cref="GroupId"/>.
    22	///     </para>
    23	/// </remarks>
    24	public record PosAlign : Pos
    25	{
    26	    /// <summary>
    27	    ///     The cached location. Used to store the calculated location to minimize recalculating it.
    28	    /// </summary>
    29	    internal int? _cachedLocation;
    30	
    31	    private readonly Aligner? _aligner;
    32	
    33	    /// <summary>
    34	    ///     Gets the alignment settings.
    35	    /// </summary>
    36	    public required Aligner Aligner
    37	    {
    38	        get => _aligner!;
    39	        init
    40	        {
    41	            if (_aligner is { })
    42	            {
    43	                _aligner.PropertyChanged -= Aligner_PropertyChanged;
    44	            }
    45	
    46	            _aligner = value;
    47	            _aligner.PropertyChanged += Aligner_PropertyChanged;
    48	        }
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    // TODO: PosAlign.CalculateMinDimension is a hack. Need to figure out a better way of doing this.
    52	    /// <summary>
    53	    ///     Returns the minimum size a group of views with the same <paramref name="groupId"/> can be.
    54	    /// </summary>
    55	    /// <param name="groupId"></param>
    56	    /// <param name="views"></param>
    57	    /// <param name="dimension"></param>
    58	    /// <returns></returns>
    59	    public static int CalculateMinDimension (int groupId, IReadOnlyCollection<View> views, Dimension dimension)
    60	    {
    61	        var dimensionsSum = 0;
    62	
    63	        foreach (View view in views)
    64	        {
    65	            if (!HasGroupId (view, dimension, groupId))
    66	            {
    67	                continue;
    68	            }
    69	
    70	            PosAlign? posAlign = dimension == Dimension.Width ? view.X as PosAlign : view.Y as PosAlign;
    71	
    72	            if (posAlign is { })
    73	            {
    74	                dimensionsSum += dimension == Dimension.Width ? view.Frame.Width : view.Frame.Height;
    75	            }
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        // Align
    79	        return dimensionsSum;
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    internal static bool HasGroupId (View v, Dimension dimension, int groupId) =>
    83	        dimension switch
    84	        {
    85	            Dimension.Width when v.X.Has (out PosAlign pos) => pos.GroupId == groupId,
    86	            Dimension.Height when v.Y.Has (out PosAlign pos) => pos.GroupId == groupId,
    87	            _ => false
    88	        };
    89	
    90	    /// <summary>
    91	    ///     Gets the identifier of a set of views that should be aligned together. When only a single
    92	    ///     set of views in a SuperView is aligned, setting <see cref="GroupId"/> is not needed because it defaults to 0.
    93	    /// </summary>
    94	    public int GroupId { get; init; }
    95	
    96	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    97	    public override string ToString () => $"Align(alignment={Aligner.Alignment},modes={Aligner.AlignmentModes},groupId={GroupId})";
    98	
    99	    internal override int Calculate (int superviewDimension, Dim dim, View us, Dimension dimension)
   100	    {
   101	        if (_cachedLocation.HasValue && Aligner.ContainerSize == superviewDimension && !us.NeedsLayout)
   102	        {
   103	            return _cachedLocation.Value;
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        List<View> groupViews = us.SuperView is null ? [us] : us.SuperView!.SubViews.Snapshot ().Where (v => HasGroupId (v, dimension, GroupId)).ToList ();
   107	
   108	        AlignAndUpdateGroup (GroupId, groupViews, dimension, superviewDimension);
   109	
   110	        if (_cachedLocation.HasValue)
   111	        {
   112	            return _cachedLocation.Value;
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        return 0;
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    internal override int GetAnchor (int width) => _cachedLocation ?? 0 - width;
   119	
   120	    /// <summary>
   121	    ///     Aligns the views in <paramref name="views"/> that have the same group ID as <paramref name="groupId"/>.
   122	    ///     Updates each view's cached _location.
   123	    /// </summary>
   124	    /// <param name="groupId"></param>
   125	    /// <param name="views"></param>
   126	    /// <param name="dimension"></param>
   127	    /// <param name="size"></param>
   128	    private static void AlignAndUpdateGroup (int groupId, IList<View> views, Dimension dimension, int size)
   129	    {
   130	        List<int> dimensionsList = new ();
   131	
   132	        // PERF: If this proves a perf issue, consider caching a ref to this list in each item
   133	        List<PosAlign?> posAligns = views.Where (v => HasGroupId (v, dimension, groupId))
   134	                                         .Select (v => dimension == Dimension.Width ? v.X as PosAlign : v.Y as PosAlign)
   135	                                         .ToList ();
   136	
   137	        // PERF: We iterate over viewsInGroup multiple times here.
   138	
   139	        Aligner? firstInGroup = null;
   140	
   141	        // Update the dimensionList with the sizes of the views
   142	        for (var index = 0; index < posAligns.Count; index++)
   143	        {
   144	            if (posAligns [index] is null)
   145	            {
   146	                continue;
   147	            }
   148	            firstInGroup ??= posAligns [index]!.Aligner;
   149	
   150	            dimensionsList.Add (dimension == Dimension.Width
   151	                                    ? views [index].Width.Calculate (0, size, views [index], dimension)
   152	                                    : views [index].Height.Calculate (0, size, views [index], dimension));
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        if (firstInGroup is null)
   156	        {
   157	            return;
   158	        }
   159	
   160	        // Update the first item in the group with the new container size.
   161	        firstInGroup.ContainerSize = size;
   162	
   163	        // Align
   164	        int [] locations = firstInGroup.Align (dimensionsList.ToArray ());
   165	
   166	        // Update the cached location for each item
   167	        for (int posIndex = 0, locIndex = 0; posIndex < posAligns.Count; posIndex++)
   168	        {
   169	            if (posAligns [posIndex] is { })
   170	            {
   171	                posAligns [posIndex]!._cachedLocation = locations [locIndex++];
   172	            }
   173	        }
   174	    }
   175	
   176	    internal override bool ReferencesOtherViews () => true;
   177	
   178	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   179	    internal override bool DependsOnSuperViewContentSize => true;
   180	
   181	    private void Aligner_PropertyChanged (object? sender, PropertyChangedEventArgs e) => _cachedLocation = null;
   182	}

   178	    public void LeftButtonPressed_On_NotActivated_Activates ()
   179	    {
   180	        // Arrange
   181	        VirtualTimeProvider time = new ();
   182	        using IApplication app = Application.Create (time);
   183	        app.Init (DriverRegistry.Names.ANSI);
   184	        IRunnable runnable = new Runnable ();
   185	
   186	        var optionSelector = new OptionSelector ();
   187	        List<string> options = ["Option1", "Option2"];
   188	        optionSelector.Labels = options;
   189	
   190	        ((View)runnable).Add (optionSelector);
   191	        app.Begin (runnable);
   192	
   193	        CheckBox checkBox = optionSelector.SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().First (cb => cb.Title == "Option2");
   194	        Assert.Equal (0, optionSelector.Value);
   195	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.Checked, optionSelector.SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().First (cb => cb.Title == "Option1").Value);
   196	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.UnChecked, checkBox.Value);
   197	
   198	        app.InjectMouse (new Mouse { ScreenPosition = checkBox.Frame.Location, Flags = MouseFlags.LeftButtonPressed });
   199	        Assert.Equal (0, optionSelector.Value);
   200	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.Checked, optionSelector.SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().First (cb => cb.Title == "Option1").Value);
   201	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.UnChecked, checkBox.Value);
   202	
   203	        app.InjectMouse (new Mouse { ScreenPosition = checkBox.Frame.Location, Flags = MouseFlags.LeftButtonReleased });
   204	        Assert.Equal (1, optionSelector.Value);
   205	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.Checked, checkBox.Value);
   206	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.UnChecked, optionSelector.SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().First (cb => cb.Title == "Option1").Value);
   207	    }

   250	    // Claude - Opus 4.6
   251	    /// <summary>
   252	    ///     MINIMAL REPRO: OptionSelector inside a Shortcut with Application context.
   253	    ///     LeftButtonReleased on "C" checkbox propagates to Shortcut (CheckBox doesn't handle it),
   254	    ///     Shortcut dispatches down to OptionSelector. Value should change to 2 ("C"), not Cycle to 1.
   255	    /// </summary>
   256	    [Fact]
   257	    public void OptionSelector_In_Shortcut_MouseClick_Selects_Correct_Item ()
   258	    {
   259	        // Need Application context for focus propagation (LeftButtonPressed sets focus)
   260	        VirtualTimeProvider time = new ();
   261	        using IApplication app = Application.Create (time);
   262	        app.Init (DriverRegistry.Names.ANSI);
   263	        IRunnable runnable = new Runnable ();
   264	
   265	        OptionSelector optionSelector = new () { Labels = ["A", "B", "C"] };
   266	        Shortcut shortcut = new () { Key = Key.F5, CommandView = optionSelector };
   267	
   268	        ((View)runnable).Add (shortcut);
   269	        app.Begin (runnable);
   270	
   271	        Assert.Equal (0, optionSelector.Value);
   272	
   273	        // Find "C" checkbox (index 2)
   274	        CheckBox checkBoxC = optionSelector.SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().First (cb => cb.Title == "C");
   275	
   276	        // Simulate: LeftButtonPressed (sets focus) then LeftButtonReleased (triggers Activate on Shortcut)
   277	        Point pos = checkBoxC.FrameToScreen ().Location;
   278	        app.InjectMouse (new Mouse { ScreenPosition = pos, Position = pos, Flags = MouseFlags.LeftButtonPressed });
   279	        app.InjectMouse (new Mouse { ScreenPosition = pos, Position = pos, Flags = MouseFlags.LeftButtonReleased });
   280	
   281	        // Assert: Value should be 2 ("C"), not 1 (Cycle from 0)
   282	        Assert.Equal (2, optionSelector.Value);
   283	    }
   284	
   285	    // Claude - Opus 4.6
   286	    /// <summary>
   287	    ///     OptionSelector inside a Shortcut. LeftButtonClicked (which CheckBox handles) on a
   288	    ///     non-selected checkbox. This is the event that the real driver synthesizes after
   289	    ///     Pressed+Released. If this fails, the Shortcut dispatch is intercepting it.
   290	    /// </summary>
   291	    [Fact]
   292	    public void OptionSelector_In_Shortcut_LeftButtonClicked_Selects_Correct_Item ()
   293	    {
   294	        OptionSelector optionSelector = new () { Labels = ["A", "B", "C"] };
   295	        Shortcut shortcut = new () { Key = Key.F5, CommandView = optionSelector };
   296	        shortcut.Layout ();
   297	
   298	        Assert.Equal (0, optionSelector.Value);
   299	
   300	        CheckBox checkBoxC = optionSelector.SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().First (cb => cb.Title == "C");
   301	
   302	        // LeftButtonClicked — this is what CheckBox binds to Command.Activate
   303	        Mouse mouse = new () { Position = checkBoxC.Frame.Location, Flags = MouseFlags.LeftButtonClicked };
   304	        checkBoxC.NewMouseEvent (mouse);
   305	
   306	        Assert.Equal (2, optionSelector.Value);
   307	    }

   326	    public void Values_NonSequential_ShouldWorkCorrectly ()
   327	    {
   328	        // Arrange
   329	        OptionSelector optionSelector = new ();
   330	        List<string> options = ["Option _1", "Option _2", "Option _3"];
   331	        List<int> values = [0, 1, 5];
   332	
   333	        optionSelector.Labels = options;
   334	        optionSelector.Values = values;
   335	
   336	        // Act & Assert
   337	        Assert.Equal (values, optionSelector.Values);
   338	        Assert.Equal (options, optionSelector.Labels);
   339	
   340	        // Verify that the Value property updates correctly
   341	        optionSelector.Value = 5;
   342	        Assert.Equal (5, optionSelector.Value);
   343	
   344	        // Verify that the CheckBox states align with the non-sequential Values
   345	        CheckBox selectedCheckBox = optionSelector.SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().First (cb => optionSelector.GetCheckBoxValue (cb) == 5);
   346	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.Checked, selectedCheckBox.Value);
   347	
   348	        CheckBox unselectedCheckBox = optionSelector.SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().First (cb => optionSelector.GetCheckBoxValue (cb) == 0); // Index 0 corresponds to value 0
   349	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.UnChecked, unselectedCheckBox.Value);
   350	    }

   462	    public void FocusedItem_DoesNotChangeValue ()
   463	    {
   464	        OptionSelector optionSelector = new ();
   465	        List<string> options = ["Option1", "Option2", "Option3"];
   466	
   467	        optionSelector.Labels = options;
   468	        optionSelector.Value = 0; // First option is selected
   469	        optionSelector.SetFocus (); // Set focus to optionSelector
   470	        optionSelector.Layout ();
   471	
   472	        // Move cursor to second checkbox
   473	        optionSelector.FocusedItem = 1;
   474	
   475	        // Value should not change, only focus moves
   476	        Assert.Equal (0, optionSelector.Value);
   477	        Assert.Equal (1, optionSelector.FocusedItem);
   478	
   479	        CheckBox [] checkBoxes = optionSelector.SubViews.OfType<CheckBox> ().ToArray ();
   480	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.Checked, checkBoxes [0].Value);
   481	        Assert.Equal (CheckState.UnChecked, checkBoxes [1].Value);
   482	        Assert.True (checkBoxes [1].HasFocus);
   483	    }

   486	    // Per OptionSelector spec: Space key cycles to next option
   487	    [Fact]
   488	    public void OptionSelector_Command_Activate_ForwardsToFocusedCheckBox ()
   489	    {
   490	        OptionSelector optionSelector = new ();
   491	        optionSelector.Labels = ["Option1", "Option2"];
   492	        optionSelector.BeginInit ();
   493	        optionSelector.EndInit ();
   494	        optionSelector.SetFocus ();
   495	
   496	        Assert.Equal (0, optionSelector.Value);
   497	
   498	        // Activate should DispatchDown to the focused CheckBox, triggering Cycle
   499	        optionSelector.InvokeCommand (Command.Activate);
   500	
   501	        Assert.Equal (1, optionSelector.Value);
   502	
   503	        optionSelector.Dispose ();
   504	    }

   506	    // Claude - Opus 4.5
   507	    // Behavior documented in docfx/docs/command.md - View Command Behaviors table
   508	    // This test verifies current behavior which may change per issue #4473
   509	    [Fact]
   510	    public void OptionSelector_Command_Accept_RaisesAccepting ()
   511	    {
   512	        OptionSelector optionSelector = new ();
   513	        optionSelector.Labels = ["Option1", "Option2"];
   514	        var acceptingFired = false;
   515	
   516	        optionSelector.Accepting += (_, e) =>
   517	                                    {
   518	                                        acceptingFired = true;
   519	                                        e.Handled = true;
   520	                                    };
   521	
   522	        bool? result = optionSelector.InvokeCommand (Command.Accept);
   523	
   524	        Assert.True (acceptingFired);
   525	        Assert.True (result);
   526	
   527	        optionSelector.Dispose ();
   528	    }
